### Round 5 - Canadian Grand Prix
*Date: 1988-06-12*

#### Qualifying Results

| Driver | Constructor | Grid | Starting Elo | Change | New Elo | vs Teammate |

### Round 10 - Hungarian Grand Prix
*Date: 1988-08-07*

#### Qualifying Results

| Driver | Constructor | Grid | Starting Elo | Change | New Elo | vs Teammate |

### Round 12 - Italian Grand Prix
*Date: 1988-09-11*
